<date>1617456949244< /date><rating>1<//rating>< Review>
On January 14, 2021 I ordered a Ventura real flame fire table from Starfire. Their representative told me that the table was in stock and would be shipped on January 31.  I was told that since they were in stock there would be no problem filling the order. I selected the table and Starfire because I was told that this table was in stock and ready to go with no waiting. I paid for the table in full. The 31st came and went with no word from Starfire. After calling them I found out that the fire table was on back order. I was told that the table would be in on March 31.  Two weeks before the 31st I called Starfire and was assured the table would be in and would be delivered within a couple of days from the 31st and probably would be in and delivered before that date. This date came and went and still no table.  I just found out after checking their website that the table is again on back order and is now expected for April 14.  I have been strung along for nearly 3 months with no end in sight.  There is zero communication from Starfire when the product goes on back order. A phone call or even an email would be appreciated. I would not recommend this company and regret spending nearly $2,000 on this table.< /Review>

< Review>
Absolutely 5 stars for the beautiful scenery!! Wish I would have taken more pictures! The seating is made up of concrete with wooden backings, not the most comfortable but it wasn't completely terrible. Lots of restrooms available for use, bring a hat, sunblock, or other form of retreat from the sun on those beautiful sunny California days. They do have a snack bar available which is really nice and convenient.  Went to an actual play years ago here but just recently went for Easter Service so I can't remember if they have other vendors all the time or not, there were lots of booths set up at the entrance so seems like they may have regulars.< /Review>

<Name>Reggie Bugmuncher</Name><Time>1525705763007< /Time><rating>5< /rating>< Review>
I just moved to this area and for months had seen signs for Ramona. I had to know what this was about, other than how long it had been around, I didn't do too much homework.  It was EVERYTHING. The moment you get out of the parking lot it kinda has a renn faire feel, like you're going to be totally submerged in something cool. The entire thing is outdoors- bring sunscreen, a hat and maybe a coat or blankie. I haven't been here for a concert yet but it looks like there are cool packages. The actual Ramona show was stunning and I have no idea how they pull off the amazing sounds and wrangling a cast that big, and with so many kids. As an entertainer I was Blown Away.< /Review>

1527551614267< /time>
<Rating>5</Rating>< Response>
None</Response>
<GmapID>0x80db6fa8776245a5:0xf43d41204f938279</GmapID>< text>
I've been to many plays!! Several of them have been out of doors. None can compare with the quality of this amazing performance at the Ramona Bowl in Hemet, California.  Ramona is the lead actress in the play which bears her name. The play is set in a remarkably beautiful natural ampitheater which must cover at least 30 or more acres. The audience of 600 occupies the seats on the south side of the ampitheater. The action of the play occurs in the valley and continues high up the hillside above the level of the audience.  The play is the longest running outdoor play in America. It has an international reputation, so people from many countries have attended the play.  Ramona is a MUST SEE event. I have attended eight times, and it never gets old.<//text>

< review>
Clem's has a great selection of beer, wine, and liquor plus a delicious deli with quality sandwiches.  The staff is very friendly and will answer any questions you might have.  The beer selection varies from common to rare brews, including some beers from previous years (great for finding aged stouts).

The deli has a good selection and he quality is on point.  You can also take it next door to the tasting room they have, which was perfect.< /review>

<Text>This bottle shop features one of the best selections of beer around, particularly for European offerings.  I often find myself on the hunt for classic examples of European beer styles that aren't particularly common in these parts, and Clem's is pretty consistently the most likely to deliver.  Freshness can sometimes be an issue, as many of the bottles are warm-stored and some of the beers probably don't turn over very quickly, and it would be nice if the beers were a bit better organized, which would help make them easier to find. <userid>108685370139018629938<//userid><Review>Clem's Bottle House has a lunch counter featuring sandwiches made with Boar's Head deli meats and cheeses nestled inside a liquor store in Kensington on Adams Avenue.

Clem's fresh hot sandwiches are made to order and are of consistently fine quality regardless of who is preparing them. My favorite is probably the "Egg Salad," which is of the creamy and chunky variety on toasted rye bread, with lettuce and pepperjack cheese. Be forewarned, however, that they do tend to annoyingly run out of egg salad by early afternoon on the weekends. The egg salad has a touch of sweetness, but will mostly be savored for its bright, fresh flavors.

When I don't order the Egg Salad, I order the "Sledgehammer." This sandwich is not just a pretty name, it also delivers the goods with hot ham, bacon, and cheddar cheese on an onion roll or french roll. I recommend having it with the onion roll, lettuce, onions, pepperoncini, mayo, and mustard. The Sledgehammer is a well put-together sandwich that is as filling and tasty as it sounds.

All sandwiches come with a pickle spear on the side. There is no seating inside the store, though there are four small tables outside.<//Review>< Rating>
4< /Rating>

< Text>
I am a 59 year old man who has been living with the HIV virus for at least 35 years, when the first blood test to detect and identify the virus was discovered,1984. I tested HIV positive then at the age of 24, and I was subsequently diagnosed with AIDS in 1992.
Living with the HIV virus for so long has altered my facial features. Weather by the disease or from the medication to treat the disease, my face became more and more gaunt, my cheeks more sunken in, and my facial bones, especially my cheek bones, became very pronounced. I had lipodistrophy. My body  could not maintain or produce healthy facial fat tissue. I was very self conscience of my appearance and it effected my self esteem.
Dr. MacGregor, the friendly and welcoming staff of the front desk, and the
warm sensitivity of the  professional personable assistance, make my appointments comfortable and efficient. The consistent and understandable communication with me and with each other as a team is excellent.
I just had my fourth treatment yesterday, replacing and stimulating the collagen in my face. I became tearful when I first saw my reflection in the mirror after the treatment. My face is now significantly more full and my bone structure is not as protruding and pronounced.The cumulative effect of the treatments have been dramatic for me. I am very pleased.
The good works of Dr. MacGregor and the staff have increased my self esteem,  given me more confidence, and has added to my social life.  Today, I am a happier and healthier looking me.
Thank you,
George< /Text>
